<p>1569. <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">obelisque</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">obeliscus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:obelisk.html>obelisk</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀβελίσκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obelískos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀβελός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obelós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:needle.html>needle</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a> (27521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">odieus</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">odiōsus</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">odium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hate.html>hate</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>more</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:most.html>most</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:odious.html>odious</a></b>)

class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ūra-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ferriferous <a href = vnd.unilang:sand.html>sand</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ofer.html>ofer</a> (102274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*uber</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*upér</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> comparative <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i>*upo</i>.
</p><p><i>Germanic cognates:</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:saxon.html>Saxon</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">oƀar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ubar</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">über</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">yfir</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">över</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language"><a href = vnd.unilang:gothic.html>Gothic</a></a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌿𐍆𐌰𐍂</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ufar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p><i>Indo-European cognates:</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὑπέρ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hupér</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:super.html>super</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a></i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language"><a href = vnd.unilang:welsh.html>Welsh</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">gor-</i>).
</p>
